## ğŸ› ï¸ What Weâ€™re Doing

## ğŸ§™ Notion API TL;DR

### Step 1: Get a Notion Integration
- Go to [Notion Integrations](https://www.notion.com/my-integrations)
- Create new integration â†’ Give it access to the relevant workspace
- Copy the **API token** it gives you

### Step 2: Share Your Database with the Integration
- Go to your `Clara Loop Archive` database in Notion
- Click "Share" â†’ Invite your integration (youâ€™ll see its name show up)

---

### Step 3: Write the Script (Node.js Example)

```js
// install packages
// npm install @notionhq/client fs

const { Client } = require("@notionhq/client");
const fs = require("fs");
const path = require("path");

// init Notion
const notion = new Client({ auth: process.env.NOTION_KEY });
const databaseId = process.env.NOTION_DB_ID;

// read files
const loopFolder = "./loops"; // folder with .md or .txt files

async function createPageFromLoop(filePath) {
  const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8");

  const titleMatch = content.match(/Loop (\d+): (.*)/);
  const loopNum = titleMatch ? titleMatch[1] : "???";
  const loopTitle = titleMatch ? titleMatch[2] : path.basename(filePath);

  await notion.pages.create({
    parent: { database_id: databaseId },
    properties: {
      Name: {
        title: [{ text: { content: `Loop ${loopNum}: ${loopTitle}` } }],
      },
      LoopNumber: {
        number: parseInt(loopNum),
      },
      Status: {
        select: { name: "Imported" },
      },
    },
    children: [
      {
        object: "block",
        type: "paragraph",
        paragraph: { text: [{ type: "text", text: { content } }] },
      },
    ],
  });

  console.log(`âœ… Imported: Loop ${loopNum}`);
}

// go through all files
fs.readdirSync(loopFolder).forEach((file) => {
  if (file.endsWith(".md") || file.endsWith(".txt")) {
    createPageFromLoop(path.join(loopFolder, file));
  }
});
```

---

### Step 4: Run It
Set your environment variables (`NOTION_KEY` and `NOTION_DB_ID`) or just hardcode them if youâ€™re living dangerously.

```bash
node importLoops.js
```

Boom. Loop pages show up in your Notion like ghosts coming home.
